	var CopyServerIP = (function() {
		var $copyip = $('[data-toggle="copyip"]');
		// Init
		function init($copyip) {
			var clipboard = new ClipboardJS('[data-toggle="copyip"]');
			clipboard.on("success", function(e) {
				swal.fire({
					title: lang.alert_title_success,
					text: lang.alert_message_server_address_copied,
					type: "success",
					confirmButtonColor: "#02b875",
					confirmButtonText: lang.alert_btn_ok
				});
			});
		}
		if ($copyip.length) {
			$copyip.each(function() {
				init($(this));
			});
		}
	})();
</script>

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const loggedInUser = localStorage.getItem('brutalNW_loggedInUser');
    const userDisplay = document.getElementById('userDisplay');
    const userAction = document.getElementById('userAction');
    const userMenuTrigger = document.getElementById('userMenuTrigger');
    const userDropdown = document.getElementById('userDropdown');
    const logoutBtn = document.getElementById('logoutBtn');
    const userPhoto = document.getElementById('userPhoto');

    function toggleDropdown(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        userDropdown.classList.toggle('hidden');
    }

    if (loggedInUser) {
        userDisplay.textContent = loggedInUser;
        userAction.textContent = 'HoÅŸ Geldin!';
        userPhoto.style.display = 'block';
        userMenuTrigger.href = '#';
        userMenuTrigger.style.cursor = 'pointer';

        // Dropdown toggle for both username and photo
        userMenuTrigger.addEventListener('click', toggleDropdown);
        userPhoto.addEventListener('click', toggleDropdown);

        // Ã‡Ä±kÄ±ÅŸ yap
        logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            if (confirm('Ã‡Ä±kÄ±ÅŸ yapmak istediÄŸinizden emin misiniz?')) {
                localStorage.removeItem('brutalNW_loggedInUser');
                location.reload();
            }
        });

        // Dropdown dÄ±ÅŸÄ±na tÄ±klayÄ±nca kapat
        document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            if (!userMenuTrigger.contains(e.target) && !userDropdown.contains(e.target) && !userPhoto.contains(e.target)) {
                userDropdown.classList.add('hidden');
            }
        });
    } else {
        userDisplay.textContent = "Misafir";
        userAction.textContent = 'GiriÅŸ Yapmak Ä°Ã§in Steve TÄ±klayÄ±n';
        document.getElementById('userPhoto').style.display = 'block';
        userMenuTrigger.style.cursor = 'pointer';
        userMenuTrigger.addEventListener('click', function() {
            window.location.href = 'login.html';
        });
        userAction.style.cursor = 'pointer';
        userAction.addEventListener('click', function() {
            window.location.href = 'login.html';
        });
    }
});
</script>
